# Funder Ingestion Tracker

This document tracks the progress of adding new funders to OpenAlex.

## Status Key

Aligned with the 9-step ladder in `how-to-add-a-funder-v2.md`:

- **Step 0**: Look up funder_id in OpenAlex
- **Step 1**: Download data and upload to S3
- **Step 2**: Create Databricks notebook
- **Step 3**: Add to CreateFunderSourcedAwards / CreateAwards
- **Step 4**: Commit and push (notebook ready; awaiting admin run)
- **Step 5**: Human runs the per-funder notebook (inserts into `openalex_awards_raw`)
- **Step 6**: Verify the data
- **Step 7**: RefreshWorkAwards merge gate (folds raw into combined `openalex_awards` + `work_awards`)
- **Step 8**: Wire notebook into the CreateFunderSourcedAwards bundle
- **Step 9 (pending ES sync)**: In `openalex_awards`; awaiting the single batch-wide Sync Awards to Elasticsearch run to go live in the API
- **Complete**: Fully integrated into OpenAlex (live in the API after ES sync)
- **DUPLICATE** / **BLOCKED**: tombstone for a row superseded by another, or work blocked at the noted step

---

Fetched via plain HTTP from AMEDfind's undocumented search API `POST /amed/web/api/get/list` (searchKind=paging, start/limit=500). The ONLY non-obvious requirement is the front-end header `x-request-origin: amedfind_web` — without it the API returns empty 400 regardless of body (this header, NOT a browser/TLS fingerprint, is the gate; verified by capturing the app's own request). No Playwright/browser needed. Each `data[].themeBasic[0]` row carries the full record: entrusterThemeNo (stable per-project id, =detail route), themeNo, themeName, jigyo (事業=funder_scheme), institution, researcherName+job (PI), allStartDate/allEndDate (FULL ISO dates), totalBudget (課題への総配分額 in 千円 → ×1000 JPY), themeOverview (description). **Full run 2026-06-04: 11,055 rows uploaded to s3://openalex-ingest/awards/amed/amed_projects.parquet** (6.35MB). Coverage: title/program/PI/institution 100%, amount 92.9% (§6.7 NOT waived — newest current-FY projects have totalBudget 0 until allocated), dates 99.4%, description 90.2%; years 2002-2025; total JPY 1.50T. Japanese PI names verbatim in family_name, given_name NULL. provenance='amed_amedfind', priority **207** (206 was claimed by ICMR HMSC via OneDrive sync mid-task; re-verify free slot at commit).
